<Pics>None<//Pics><review>I have to admit, I always thought I was one who couldn't handle spice...even the chili dust from eating popcorn chicken would set my mouth ablaze. With that being said, I never really enjoyed hot chicken sandwiches to it's full potential; I always opted for 'non-spicy'. My life changed 180 when I decided to give Chicken as Cluck's Nashville hot chicken sandwich a try...with ACTUAL spice! Oh My Goodness, the sandwich was sooo good! Although it was mild-medium spicy, it was a just the right amount spice that just meets my threshold. The chicken meat was very moist and the brioche bun was the perfect carrier. I gobbled it up and enjoyed every bite. To accompany the sandwich, I ordered sweet potato fries, which have a panko batter coating. This is great as the fries are extra crispy. Who doesn't love a good crunch?!

I'm glad that Chicken as Cluck was my gateway sandwich to the Nashville hot chicken sandwich world.< /review>< user_name>
Rene Beck< /user_name>

< Review>
First time at Mas Taco Bar. The staff was friendly and the food was fresh. I ordered the drunken chicken bowl with brown rice. I asked about the rice - no white or wild rice is offered. The chicken was tender and the food was hot without having the bowl heated to 1000 degrees as with most Mexican restaurants. It has a sports bar feel with many screens either showing football or the world series. Casual dress code. The music was modern pop sound track.< /Review>

< review>
AMAZING. Food was absolutely delicious (secret taco and blackened salmon taco) and the service from Janelle (server), John (server/bartender), and Brandon (busser) were top notch. Give these employees a raise seriously.

I work in the service industry (Marriott Sales) and I am all about the delivery, service, taste and overall experience/vibe of an establishment and Mas Tacos in Folsom NAILED it. I want to work there now. Haha

This is a direct reflection of management and Colin delivered. Spoke with him briefly and he is a great guy. It seems as though he gives his employees the ability to let their unique and individualistic personalities show through their professional but excellent service.

Props to you guys! Price was right on point too. I would 100% go back. (I went for lunch and early dinner both in the same day) that should prove my point. They have something special going in Folsom. Early PM and late PM shifts were great. Thank you Mas Tacos. Y'all rock!</review>

We arrived and were the only ones at the time.  The hostess said it would be about 5 minutes for a table.  About 20 minutes later,  she came to seat us all the time handing out to-go orders. Finally seated and about 10 minutes later,  the waitress shows up and took our drink orders.  Awhile later,  she comes back and sets 2 margaritas in front of us. The waitress came back and we ordered some food to go home with and a different drink while waiting.  The dragonberry mojito turned out so bad we left them on the table. Again,  we have to wait for the waitress to bring the tab to us. It appears she had too many tables for one person.  Not going back.<//review>

< review>
Excellent service! Started out by ordering a round of Cadillac Margaritas - best idea ever! They were strong, wonderfully tasty and delicious! The appetizers also did not disappoint. Wonderful braised beef short ribs with pickled onion in a buttery flaky pie crust - the tostones were a packages of heaven! However if you prefer a Kickstart appetizer, do yourself a favor and order the Habanero Fire Balls! Warm, gooey, and spicy!
Oh yeah, didn't we came here for the tacos? Always ask about the secret taco, this one was roasted seasonal vegetables. Just perfection! Notables for our group was Braised short rib, Battered Fish, Banh mi Shrimp, Pork Belly, and Vietnamese Pork - my favorite! Never disappointed going here - the food is always fresh and creative! Love Mas Taco!< /review>

< Text>
Went there to try the place for the first time last Thursday and sat at the bar as I often do because service is usually better. Not at this place. I sat there and sat there and finally waved a bartender down to get a drink. In fact, I had to wave the bartenders down every time I wanted to order something. They were a little busy, but not bad and there were three bartenders working. When I got my drink, there was something floating in it. I waved the bartender down (again) and he quickly apologized and got me a new drink. The thing is, he asked me if I wanted a new straw.  Yes, of course. If you're replacing a drink because something gross happened in the preparation, I think a good bartender would start with a clean glass and new straw.

We tried several of the food items, starting with ceviche. Utterly tasteless. This did not bode well for any of the other items we tried. The tacos looked good, but were completely bland. It is like they use a Star Trek replicator to prepare the food. They know what it's supposed to look like, but have no idea how it should taste. Pretty bad for a place with "tacos" in the name.< /Text>

<rate>5</rate><review>After a long day of moving, 4 adults were soooo hungry! But with gluten free and vegetarian among us, we had a hard time finding a place we could all enjoy.
Luckily, my husband remembered me saying months ago that I wanted to Mas Taco Bar. It also happened to be the birthday of one of our party, so we went in looking for a lively vibe, good food and cocktails.
We we NOT disappointed at all!! It was a Saturday night, and the place was poppin! We were able to get a seat right away, but I think a wait started just after us.
We had a great meal...the Mas Marguerita is awesome and we had many. The vibe was fun and loud with lots of laughter throughout the restaurant.
Meat, fish, chicken, vegan and vegetarian options and since their corm tortillas are DELISH it works for GF peeps too. Their corn shells totally changed my mind about I only liked flour tortillas btw.
All ingredients are FRESH and bright and did I mention delicious?
NOTE: Tacos are $3 each, but they are street tacos meaning tiny.
WARNING: This place can get costly. The tacos are addictive and an average adult male will eat anywhere from 6-10 to be filled. The drinks and oh yeah...the GUAC and CHIPS is INSANE so you will definitely want to have that (free chip refills...and when you try them you will definitely want refills)...and don't miss dessert...the price can sneak up on you.
That said, we had a great meal, great service, and a great time so well worth it.
TAKE AWAY: Awesome place for a family style, hang out, eat and drink for a couple hours night out< /review><pics>None< /pics><response>None< /response><Gmap_id>0x809ae5938f574175:0x4e5f66c30609b6cc< /Gmap_id></record>

< Text>
Remember these names; Staci, Desari, Jamie and Sidney.  While I suspect the rest of the staff here is far above par, these people are AWESOME!

I'm one of those people who have a tricky genetic blood disease.  If improperly treated, I can bleed out. This makes me very concerned and hyper vigilant in my medical care. So many urgent care facilities haven't bothered to educate themselves before examining me or deciding my treatment.  I haven't been happy with the quality of the urgent care facilities in this area. From the moment I went into the doors of those other places, it's been all down hill.  Because of this, I was extremely tense when I entered the doors of REDLANDS URGENT CARE CENTER.

OH MY GOSH!  I literally have used urgent care facilities all through the United States. REDLANDS URGENT CARE CENTER is far the best place I've been. The moment I went through the door I was greeted. The receptionist quickly asked me questions, acted on those answers and enrolled me as a patient.  There was only one other person in the lobby. She said she was always given amazing care there.  They took her immediately.

As soon as I signed my name, I was taken to an exam room. My vitals were taken and the nurse practitioner immediately came in.  She was able to identify the cause of my discomfort right away. She clearly explained it and I was reassured she understood the critical issues in my care caused by my genetic blood disease. As I kept asking questions to reassure myself that I wasn't being given medication which might prove very dangerous to me, she remained patient, positive and informative. I felt like she was content to stand right there as long as I needed her!  Yes, she chose medications safe for me to take and I feel so much better today.

The facility was pleasantly decorated. It was clean, organized and smelled fresh. The furniture was tasteful and in good repair.

On a scale of one to ten with ten being the best......this business and the people taking care of me were easily 1,000 each.  They are what those one to tens are trying to be when they grow up.

I highly recommend this business.  Since I have to go 71 miles one way to USC for my medical appointments and scheduled care, I was eager to find a safe place for me to go for a cold, a sore throat, etc.   I'm so happy to finally identify the type of care I've been looking for.

Thank you REDLANDS URGENT CARE CENTER and a very grateful thank you to Jamie, Sidney, Desari and Staci!<//Text>

She removed the additional chicken charge from the bill (an honest oversight as we recently updated our menu and computer system).\n\nIt's not Renee's fault that our policy is not to do more than 2 split checks - and many other restaurants that I know of have enacted similar policies.  [The businees reasons are simple - each swipe of a credit or debit card costs us about $0.50 (this is why the Calco and Arco gas stations charge you 40 cents to use a debit card), plus the additional work and time and effort to do so. So splitting a check 6 ways takes my server 5 minutes and costs me $3.00 instead of 50 cents and 1 minute.  In the era of slim profit margins every cost matters, and I'd rather have my server spending 5 minutes on taking care of his/her tables rather than standing at the credit card terminal and computer system.  Plus now it is easy to send other people money if you dont have cash - Zelle, Venmo, PayPal, PopMoney, Google Wallet, Apple Pay, etc. are all free and nearly instant.]\n\nThe comment about eating at the Mexican restaurant instead was inappropriate, and she apologized to me for saying that, and I'm passing on the apology to you. It just wasn't out of the blue that she came up with that.\n\nFinally, but very disturbing to me, is the fact that some in your group left without paying their bill (which Renee did split 6 ways at the end to try and make peace).  Three of the 6 bills were paid (2 credit cards and one cash), but the other three guest books were empty.  I audited all our records and looked at the cameras, and it is fairly obvious they were not paid.  It is one thing to not tip a server because of poor service (I completely understand this), but to walk out without paying is stealing from me. The whole experience was very relaxing.  I think I actually dozed off a little during my treatment.  I left with my skin feeling refreshed and clean.  It's been 3 days since my facial and I can honestly say my acne did shrink (not totally gone yet but hopefully soon!)  Sue was nice and easy to talk to during my facial.  I highly recommend her!

Parking tip: Park in the residential neighborhood on Delongpre and Flores and walk up the white stairway to the Sunset Tower Hotel.< /Text>

Like most men, my experience with salons and skin care is severely limited, long considered a realm reserved strictly for women. It is a shame that I did not venture into this world of facials earlier in life, as the results are nothing short of spectacular.

Enter Joanna Vargas, esthetician to the stars. Her signature Triple Crown Facial has opened my eyes (and pores) to the possibilities of proper skin care. I did a little research before heading over to her West Hollywood salon, just so I knew what I was getting into. The treatment called for a combo of technologies that would remove dead skin, reduce puffiness, and reshape my jawline. Sounds good to me, I could do with less puff.

Upon arrival, I was impressed with the d√©cor of the space. Located in a quaint condo just steps off 3rd Street, the feeling is that you just stepped into a gorgeous and welcoming hotel suite. The staff makes you feel right at home, as if the entire place is your private oasis for the next hour. There was a hint of perfectionism in the air with all the accents, which instilled confidence that my treatment was going to be world class.

Asia Vereline was my guide throughout this journey, and she didn‚Äôt disappoint. With a genial bedside manner, she explained the process: Microdermabrasion to exfoliate and remove dead skin, followed by a microcurrent session that stimulates and strengthens the facial muscles, and capped off with oxygen-infused therapy.

The session was relaxing, akin to a luxurious massage, and as I my face was receiving its upgrade, I dozed off a little, succumbing to the comfortable environment. At one point, Asia pulled out a mirror so I could see the instantaneous results. It was quite clear that a difference had already been made, as the redness and puffiness were completely gone.

At the conclusion of the treatment, I spent probably too much time looking in the mirror admiring the changed complexion. What a masterpiece! My skin was certainly glowing, and my jawline was more pronounced.

So fellas, put a facial down on your Christmas wish list, and let the good folks at Joanna Vargas change your mind on what it means to have a spa day.< /Text>

<time>1485715448223< /time><Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
Yesterday - Saturday (1/28/2017) - my wife and I took my elderly mother here for lunch.  We arrived about 1pm and were only people in the place until about half-way through our meal when a couple other small groups/families came in.  Ordered pot stickers, hot and sour soup and a sizzling plate dish with a mix of chicken, pork, beef, shrimp and vegetables.   Portion sizes were very generous (especially the soup) and everyone liked the flavors.  Service was also reasonably quick -- but maybe that was helped by fact we were only people there when we first arrived.   Also price seemed very reasonable.  Bill with tax came to about $30.   All in all, we will definitely be eating here again.  Maybe next time we will try the BBQ platter.<//text>

<user_id>111022786301370340046< /user_id><Pics>None<//Pics><user_name>Solomon<//user_name>< text>
This place has unique authentic Chinese food that can't be found in any other Chinese restaurants in Sonoma County. If you want to try something different from typical American Chinese food and don't want to drive out to SF, this is the go-to place. They have authentic Hong Kong style Dried Scallop Egg White Fried Rice (my favorite) and excellently prepared Singapore Rice Noodle. If you are feeling adventurous, try their Spicy/Soya Pork Ears or Tendon (Be prepared to be Spicier than other American Chinese restaurants if you ordered Spicy), Special Ham Hock and Beef Tripe with Black Bean Sauce.  In addition, they offer authentic Cantonese Hot Pot on the second floor. It's perfect if you have a part of five or more.<//text>
